1188:### 11.4.1 Controls implemented in P4
1189:
1190:The mockup shows several controls the operator can interact with. Each is either specified here with a concrete P4 implementation, or explicitly marked **decorative** so no implementation work is required.
1191:
1192:| Control | Mockup location | P4 behaviour |
1193:|---|---|---|
1194:| **Auto-refresh ("updated every 60 seconds")** | Footer copy on line 1141 of the mockup | **Real.** React Query uses `refetchInterval: 60_000` across all `/api/admin/llm-pnl/*` queries. Footer copy is accurate. |
1195:| **Refresh button** | Top-right of page header (mockup line 137) | **Real.** Manual `queryClient.invalidateQueries(['systemPnl'])` — forces immediate refetch of all P&L queries. |
1196:| **Export CSV button** | Top-right of page header (mockup line 156) | **Real, client-side only.** Clicking the button serialises the currently-visible tab's React Query cache to CSV and triggers a browser download. No new API endpoint. Implementation is a ~30-line client-side helper (`exportTabAsCsv(tab, rows)`); columns match the rendered table verbatim. Scope: the active tab's rows at the current filter/sort. |
1197:| **View all (in "Top calls by cost" header)** | Mockup line 994 | **Real, as an anchor scroll + limit bump.** Clicking sets the client-side `topCallsLimit` state from 10 to 50 and smooth-scrolls to the top of the Top-calls section. No new page, no new route. "All" means "up to 50 in the current period," not "every row ever." |
1198:| **Footer link — "Margin policies"** | Mockup line 1144 | **Decorative.** Rendered as a `<span>` styled like a link but with no `href` and no click handler. Real destination deferred — see §17. |
1199:| **Footer link — "Retention"** | Mockup line 1145 | **Decorative.** Same treatment as "Margin policies." Real destination deferred — see §17. |
1200:| **Footer link — "Billing rules"** | Mockup line 1146 | **Decorative.** Same treatment as "Margin policies." Real destination deferred — see §17. |
1201:
1202:Rationale: the mockup makes visible commitments to the operator. Refresh, Export CSV, View all, and the 60s auto-refresh are cheap to honour with client-side-only work and the mockup would feel broken without them. Admin-only footer destinations (`Margin policies`, `Retention`, `Billing rules`) would balloon P4 scope into a multi-page admin suite — decorative-for-now is the cheapest honouring of the mockup's visual intent without committing P4 to pages that don't yet exist.
1203:
1204:### 11.5 Column contracts per tab
1205:
1206:See §19 Contracts for the full TypeScript types. Column order matches the mockup verbatim. Sort directions default to cost-descending. Filter UI on every column header follows the `ColHeader` dropdown pattern.
1207:
1208:| Tab | Columns | Sort default |
1209:|---|---|---|
1210:| By Organisation | Organisation \| Subaccounts \| Requests \| Revenue \| Cost \| Profit \| Margin \| % of Revenue \| Trend | Cost desc |
1211:| By Subaccount | Subaccount \| Organisation \| Requests \| Revenue \| Cost \| Profit \| Margin \| % of Revenue | Cost desc |
1212:| By Source Type | Source Type \| Orgs \| Requests \| Revenue \| Cost \| Profit \| Margin \| % of Cost | Cost desc |
1213:| By Provider / Model | Provider \| Model \| Requests \| Revenue \| Cost \| Profit \| Margin \| Avg Latency \| Share of Cost | Cost desc |
1214:
1215:**Overhead row treatment (applied wherever an overhead row renders):**
1216:- Revenue: em-dash
1217:- Profit: negative cost, displayed in muted slate-500 with a minus sign
1218:- Margin: "overhead" badge instead of percentage
1219:- Pulled out visually with a subtle indigo background
1220:
1221:**Which tabs render overhead rows** (matches `prototypes/system-costs-page.html`):
1222:
1223:| Tab | Overhead treatment |
1224:|---|---|
1225:| By Organisation | One synthetic aggregated overhead row (labelled `Overhead · Platform background work`) that sums `system` + `analyzer` cost across every org. The By Subaccount tab slices by a different dimension; see below. |
1226:| By Subaccount | No overhead row. Subaccount grouping has no natural home for platform-wide overhead (overhead has no subaccount), so the tab renders only subaccount rows. Aggregate overhead is visible via the Platform overhead KPI card and the `By Source Type` and `By Organisation` tabs. |
1227:| By Source Type | Two overhead rows — `system` and `analyzer` — rendered as separate rows per §19.5. |
1228:| By Provider / Model | No overhead row. Platform overhead crosses provider/model lines; splitting it by provider would add noise without observability win. Aggregate overhead is visible elsewhere. |
1229:
1230:On `By Source Type`, both `system` and `analyzer` render as overhead rows per the treatment above. The schema-level split between `system` and `analyzer` (added in §6.1) is preserved here so operators can see analyzer spend at a glance instead of hiding it behind a single "System" line.
1231:
1232:**Totals row at the bottom of each table:**
1233:- Rev/Cost/Profit: summed across all visible rows including every overhead row rendered on that tab
1234:- Margin: computed as net margin (profit/revenue) or noted as "net" if including overhead rows
1235:
1236:### 11.6 Detail drawer
1237:
1238:**Opens on:** clicking any row in "Top calls by cost."
1239:
1240:**Fields shown:**
1241:- Provider request ID (copyable)
1242:- Idempotency key
1243:- Full error message + code (if non-success)
1244:- Token breakdown (input, output, cached prompt tokens)
1245:- Latency breakdown (router overhead + provider latency)
1246:- Fallback chain (JSON-decoded from the column)
1247:- Retry attempt number
1248:- `parseFailureRawExcerpt` rendered in a monospace block if non-null
1249:- Links back to: originating run (if `runId` present), job (if `sourceId` present), organisation, subaccount
1250:- "Copy as support ticket" button — formats provider_request_id + model + error into a block suitable for pasting into an Anthropic support ticket

2026-04-20T06:51:15.115978Z ERROR codex_core::tools::router: error=Exit code: 1
Wall time: 0.4 seconds
Output:
1251:
1252:**Scope note:** rich-state interactions on the drawer (filter-by-request-ID inline, keyboard nav) are **deferred** — see §17. Base drawer ships with Phase 4.
1253:
1254:### 11.7 What the page does NOT do (scope discipline)
1255:
1256:- Not a billing dashboard — no invoice generation, no payment reconciliation.
1257:- Not a forecasting tool — no "projected monthly cost" figures.
1258:- Not a per-user drill-down — user-level cost views live on the existing Usage page.
1259:- Not an anomaly alert surface — "Platform overhead >15% of revenue for 3 days" alerting is deferred (§17).
1260:- Not a replacement for the existing Usage page — that page remains the subaccount-scoped view for org admins. The P&L page is platform-admin-only.
1261:
1262:---
1263:
1264:## 12. Retention policy for `llm_requests`
1265:
1266:### 12.1 Problem
1267:
1268:`llm_requests` grows unbounded by design — it's a financial audit ledger. At steady-state with live clients, conservative estimate is 50,000–200,000 rows per month per paying org. With 10 paying orgs, that's ~2M rows/month, ~24M rows/year. Each row is ~1 KB (mostly hashes + numeric), so ~24 GB/year. Manageable but not trivial, and the indexes on this table multiply storage.
1269:
1270:**The purpose of retention is NOT cost reduction.** It is:
1271:- Faster queries on the hot path (last 90 days is what dashboards actually read).
1272:- Cleaner index rebuilds (smaller indexes rebuild faster on migration).
1273:- Operational safety: a single runaway analyzer run can't DoS the ledger.
1274:
1275:### 12.2 Decision
1276:
1277:**Keep full detail rows in `llm_requests` for `env.LLM_LEDGER_RETENTION_MONTHS` months (default 12).** After that, move rows to `llm_requests_archive` (same shape, subset of indexes).
1278:
1279:**`cost_aggregates` rollups are kept forever.** Daily rollups are tiny (one row per org per day per dimension — thousands of rows total, not millions) and power the long-term financial reports.
1280:
1281:### 12.3 `llm_requests_archive` (migration 0183)
1282:
1283:Shape: identical to `llm_requests` at migration time. Drizzle schema: share a common type shape, two Drizzle tables.
1284:
1285:Indexes: only the ones needed for occasional lookup by support/compliance:
1286:
1287:- `idempotency_key` — for proof-of-billing queries.
1288:- `provider_request_id` — for Anthropic support tickets.
1289:- `organisation_id, billing_month` — for "show me all calls for this org in 2026" support flows.
1290:
1291:**Not copied to archive:** partial indexes on `status`, `execution_phase`, `execution_id`, `feature_tag`. These are dashboard-hot; archived data doesn't need them.
1292:
1293:### 12.4 `llm-ledger-archive` job (new pg-boss job)
1294:
1295:**Files:**
1296:- `server/jobs/llmLedgerArchiveJob.ts` (new) — the job orchestration + DB transaction loop (impure).
1297:- `server/jobs/llmLedgerArchiveJobPure.ts` (new) — pure helpers extracted out of the job for testability. Exports `computeArchiveCutoff(retentionMonths, now)`.
1298:
1299:**Schedule:** nightly at 03:00 UTC (pg-boss cron).
1300:
1301:**Pure helper (`llmLedgerArchiveJobPure.ts`):**
1302:
1303:```ts
1304:/**
1305: * Cutoff for archive-eligibility: rows strictly older than `retentionMonths`
1306: * calendar months before `now` are moved to the archive table.
1307: *
1308: * `now` is injected for test determinism; the caller passes `new Date()` at
1309: * runtime. Uses `setMonth(getMonth() - n)` rather than day arithmetic so the
1310: * cutoff tracks month boundaries rather than a naive 30-day window.
1311: */
1312:export function computeArchiveCutoff(retentionMonths: number, now: Date): Date {
1313:  const cutoff = new Date(now.getTime());
1314:  cutoff.setMonth(cutoff.getMonth() - retentionMonths);
1315:  return cutoff;
1316:}
1317:```
1318:
1319:The corresponding test at `server/jobs/__tests__/ledgerArchivePure.test.ts` (§14.8a) exercises this helper directly — no DB, no mocks.
1320:
1321:**Shape (`llmLedgerArchiveJob.ts`):**
1322:
1323:```ts
1324:export async function archiveOldLedgerRows(): Promise<ArchiveResult> {
1325:  const cutoff = computeArchiveCutoff(env.LLM_LEDGER_RETENTION_MONTHS, new Date());
1326:
1327:  // Move rows in 10k-row chunks to bound transaction size.
1328:  // Postgres does NOT support `DELETE ... ORDER BY ... LIMIT` directly, so we
1329:  // pick ids with a separate SELECT first (cheap because `created_at` is indexed),
1330:  // then copy + delete those specific ids. Using `FOR UPDATE SKIP LOCKED`
1331:  // keeps the job safe under concurrent runs (though the nightly cadence
1332:  // makes concurrency very unlikely).
1333:  let totalMoved = 0;
1334:  for (;;) {
1335:    const moved = await db.transaction(async (tx) => {
1336:      const result = await tx.execute(sql`
1337:        WITH doomed AS (
1338:          SELECT id
1339:          FROM llm_requests
1340:          WHERE created_at < ${cutoff}
1341:          ORDER BY created_at
1342:          LIMIT 10000
1343:          FOR UPDATE SKIP LOCKED
1344:        ),
1345:        inserted AS (
1346:          INSERT INTO llm_requests_archive
1347:          SELECT * FROM llm_requests
1348:          WHERE id IN (SELECT id FROM doomed)
1349:          RETURNING id
1350:        )
1351:        DELETE FROM llm_requests
1352:        WHERE id IN (SELECT id FROM inserted)
1353:        RETURNING 1;
1354:      `);
1355:      return result.rowCount ?? 0;
1356:    });
1357:    totalMoved += moved;
1358:    if (moved < 10000) break;
1359:  }
1360:  return { totalMoved, cutoff };
1361:}
1362:```
1363:
1364:**Safety:**
1365:
1366:- CTE with `DELETE ... RETURNING` + `INSERT` in a single transaction means a row is either in `llm_requests` OR in `llm_requests_archive`, never both, never neither.
1367:- `ORDER BY created_at LIMIT 10000` bounds each transaction to ~10 MB.
1368:- Job is idempotent — re-running it on the same day does nothing if the first run cleared the cutoff.
1369:
1370:**Verification:**
1371:
1372:- `getCallDetail(id)` reads from both tables (UNION ALL) transparently so detail drawer works for archived rows.
1373:- `getTopCalls()` reads only `llm_requests` (the last 30 days are never archived).
1374:
1375:### 12.5 Environment + config
1376:
1377:**New env var:** `LLM_LEDGER_RETENTION_MONTHS` (default: `12`). Declared in [server/lib/env.ts](server/lib/env.ts).
1378:
1379:No admin-facing config UI — this is an infrastructure tunable, not a business decision.
1380:
1381:### 12.6 Deferred from retention (see §17)
1382:
1383:- **`llm_requests_archive` further tiering** (e.g. "after 36 months, move to cold storage or dump to S3"). Not needed until data volume justifies it.
1384:- **Per-org retention overrides.** If a client demands 5-year audit retention by contract, that's a commercial conversation handled outside this spec.
1385:
1386:---
1387:
1388:## 13. Permissions & RLS
1389:
1390:### 13.1 `llm_requests` — existing RLS state
1391:
1392:`llm_requests` is already listed in [server/config/rlsProtectedTables.ts](server/config/rlsProtectedTables.ts) as an org-scoped table with RLS enabled. The new columns added in this spec (`source_id`, `feature_tag`, `parse_failure_raw_excerpt`, `abort_reason`) do not change the RLS policy — the `organisation_id` column remains the scoping axis, and all new columns are dependent on that column for access.
1393:
1394:**No RLS migration required** for the column additions. Verify after migration 0180 lands that `verify-rls-coverage.sh` still passes.
1395:
1396:### 13.2 `llm_requests_archive` — new table RLS requirement
1397:
1398:Per §4 of the spec-authoring checklist: every new tenant-scoped table must have (1) RLS policy, (2) manifest entry, (3) route guard, (4) principal-scoped context.
1399:
1400:**Application to `llm_requests_archive`:**
1401:
1402:1. **RLS policy:** identical to `llm_requests` — rows readable only when `organisation_id = current_setting('app.organisation_id')::uuid` OR when the caller is admin-connection-scoped (admin reads bypass).
1403:2. **Manifest entry:** add `llm_requests_archive` to `server/config/rlsProtectedTables.ts` in the same migration (0183) that creates the table. `verify-rls-coverage.sh` enforces this.
1404:3. **Route guard:** no HTTP route reads the archive directly. `getCallDetail()` reads via `systemPnlService` which runs under `requireSystemAdmin` + `withAdminConnection`. If an org-scoped route needs archived data later, that requires a separate spec.
1405:4. **Principal-scoped context:** admin reads use `withAdminConnection`. No agent-execution path reads the archive.
1406:
1407:### 13.3 System P&L page — admin-scoped reads
1408:
1409:**Deliberate cross-tenant read:** the System P&L page is the one UI that reads across all organisations by design. It is gated by:
1410:
1411:- `requireSystemAdmin` middleware on every `/api/admin/llm-pnl/*` route.
1412:- `withAdminConnection` for the actual DB queries (bypasses RLS).
1413:- No other route or UI exposes this data.
1414:
1415:**Why not a new permission key?** `requireSystemAdmin` already exists and is sufficient. Introducing `system_pnl_view` would be redundant — there is no sub-role of "system admin who can see skills but not costs" that we want to express today.
1416:
1417:### 13.4 `cost_aggregates` — already covered
1418:
1419:`cost_aggregates` is already in the RLS manifest. The new `entity_type = 'source_type' | 'feature_tag'` values don't change its row shape, just add writes. No migration to RLS policy.
1420:
1421:### 13.5 System-level rows and RLS
1422:
1423:Ledger rows with `sourceType = 'system'` or `'analyzer'` still have `organisation_id` set (the organisation that initiated the analyzer run). These rows ARE subject to RLS like every other row.
1424:
1425:The exception is system rows with no attributable org — e.g. a periodic platform-wide maintenance job that spans orgs. Today, no such caller exists. If one is added, we either assign it a synthetic "platform" org UUID OR add an `organisation_id` nullable column + RLS policy extension. Out of scope for this spec.
1426:

1548:## 15. Phase sequencing (dependency graph)

1550:Each phase is a single PR. Phases land in order; no phase depends on a column/table/service created in a later phase.

1553:

Every other attribution path is unchanged.

2024:#### 19.5.2 `SourceTypeRow`
2025:
2026:**Type:** TypeScript, declared in `shared/types/systemPnl.ts`.
2027:
2028:Renders 5 rows on the `By Source Type` tab — one per distinct `sourceType` value: `agent_run`, `process_execution`, `iee`, `system`, `analyzer`. The schema-level split between `system` and `analyzer` (added in §6.1) is preserved in the UI so operators can see analyzer spend at a glance instead of hiding it behind a single "System" line.
2029:
2030:**Shape:**
2031:```ts
2032:{
2033:  sourceType: 'agent_run' | 'process_execution' | 'iee' | 'system' | 'analyzer';
2034:  label: string;                   // display label (e.g. "Agent Run", "System Background")
2035:  description: string;             // one-line description shown under the label
2036:  orgsCount: number;               // distinct organisation count contributing to this row (for billable rows); 0 for overhead rows
2037:  requests: number;
2038:  revenueCents: number | null;     // null for sourceType ∈ {'system','analyzer'} (no revenue attribution)
2039:  costCents: number;
2040:  profitCents: number;             // = revenueCents - costCents for billable rows; = -costCents for overhead rows
2041:  marginPct: number | null;        // null for overhead rows — rendered as "overhead" badge
2042:  pctOfCost: number;               // percentage of this period's total platform cost
2043:}
2044:```
2045:
2046:**Example — `system` row (platform overhead that is not analyzer work):**
2047:```ts
2048:{
2049:  sourceType: "system",
2050:  label: "System Background",
2051:  description: "Memory compile · orchestration · miscellaneous system work",
2052:  orgsCount: 0,
2053:  requests: 187319,
2054:  revenueCents: null,
2055:  costCents: 164283,
2056:  profitCents: -164283,
2057:  marginPct: null,
2058:  pctOfCost: 7.0,
2059:}
2060:```
2061:
2062:**Example — `analyzer` row:**
2063:```ts
2064:{
2065:  sourceType: "analyzer",
2066:  label: "Skill Analyzer",
2067:  description: "Classify · agent-match · cluster-recommend",
2068:  orgsCount: 0,
2069:  requests: 25718,
2070:  revenueCents: null,
2071:  costCents: 24459,
2072:  profitCents: -24459,
2073:  marginPct: null,
2074:  pctOfCost: 1.0,
2075:}
2076:```
2077:
2078:Both `system` and `analyzer` rows carry the same "overhead" treatment (null revenue, null margin, rendered as em-dashes by `PnlBySourceTypeTable.tsx`). The `system` row's description drops the word "Analyzers" — analyzer work is now its own row.
2079:
2080:**Producer:** `systemPnlService.getBySourceType()`.
2081:**Consumer:** `PnlBySourceTypeTable.tsx` renders em-dashes for null `revenueCents` and `marginPct` across both overhead rows.
2082:
2083:#### 19.5.3 `ProviderModelRow`
2084:
2085:**Type:** TypeScript, declared in `shared/types/systemPnl.ts`.
2086:
2087:**Example:**
2088:```ts
2089:{
2090:  provider: "anthropic",
2091:  model: "claude-sonnet-4-6",
2092:  requests: 412918,
2093:  revenueCents: 1843219,
2094:  costCents: 1320442,
2095:  profitCents: 522777,
2096:  marginPct: 28.4,
2097:  avgLatencyMs: 2847,            // AVG(provider_latency_ms) across the period's rows
2098:  pctOfCost: 55.7,               // percentage of this period's total platform cost
2099:}
2100:```
2101:
2102:**Nullability:** none — every row has a concrete provider+model pair.
2103:
2104:**Producer:** `systemPnlService.getByProviderModel()`.
2105:**Consumer:** `PnlByProviderModelTable.tsx`.
2106:
2107:### 19.5a `DailyTrendRow`
2108:
2109:**Type:** TypeScript, declared in `shared/types/systemPnl.ts`.
2110:
2111:**Example:**
2112:```ts
2113:{
2114:  day: "2026-04-20",           // ISO date (YYYY-MM-DD), one row per calendar day in the requested window
2115:  revenueCents: 93814,
2116:  costCents: 76121,
2117:  overheadCents: 6254,         // sum of sourceType ∈ {'system','analyzer'} cost for this day
2118:}
2119:```
2120:
2121:**Nullability:** all numeric fields default to 0 for days with no activity (not null). `day` is always present.
2122:
2123:**Series meaning on the chart:**
2124:- `revenueCents` and `costCents` are the two primary series (stacked area + line).
2125:- **Net profit** on the chart is derived client-side as `revenueCents - costCents` and is NOT sent as a separate field (overhead is already included in `costCents`, so this subtraction produces net profit directly). Keeping profit off the wire prevents drift between contract and display math.
2126:- `overheadCents` is rendered as a secondary line/area in muted indigo so operators can see platform overhead separately from the primary cost line. Including it as a field avoids a second round-trip for the chart.
2127:
2128:**Ordering:** rows are returned in ascending `day` order; consumer does not need to sort.
2129:
2130:**Producer:** `systemPnlService.getDailyTrend(days)`.
2131:**Consumer:** `PnlTrendChart.tsx`.
2132:
2133:### 19.6 `TopCallRow` + `CallDetail`
2134:
2135:**Example `TopCallRow` (billable, agent run):**
2136:```ts
2137:{
2138:  id: "row-uuid",
2139:  createdAt: "2026-04-20T14:38:22.102Z",
2140:  organisationName: "Summit Digital",
2141:  subaccountName: "Creative Ops",
2142:  marginTier: 1.40,
2143:  sourceType: "agent_run",
2144:  sourceLabel: "Agent Run",
2145:  provider: "anthropic",
2146:  model: "claude-sonnet-4-6",
2147:  tokensIn: 12843,
2148:  tokensOut: 6218,
2149:  revenueCents: 26,               // $0.2553
2150:  costCents: 18,
2151:  profitCents: 8,
2152:  status: "success",
2153:}
2154:```
2155:
2156:**Example `TopCallRow` (non-billable, analyzer overhead):**
2157:```ts
2158:{
2159:  id: "row-uuid-2",
2160:  createdAt: "2026-04-20T14:36:09.102Z",
2161:  organisationName: null,          // system/analyzer rows — rendered as "— system —" by the client
2162:  subaccountName: null,
2163:  marginTier: null,
2164:  sourceType: "analyzer",
2165:  sourceLabel: "Skill Analyzer Classify",
2166:  provider: "anthropic",
2167:  model: "claude-sonnet-4-6",
2168:  tokensIn: 8895,
2169:  tokensOut: 122,
2170:  revenueCents: null,              // null for sourceType ∈ {'system','analyzer'} — renders as em-dash
2171:  costCents: 4,
2172:  profitCents: -4,                 // = -costCents when revenueCents is null
2173:  status: "client_disconnected",
2174:}
2175:```
2176:
2177:**Nullability:** `revenueCents` is `number | null` — null for rows where `sourceType ∈ {'system','analyzer'}` because those rows are platform overhead (no revenue attribution). `organisationName`, `subaccountName`, and `marginTier` are also nullable for overhead rows. Consumer (`PnlTopCallsList.tsx`) renders em-dashes for null fields.
2178:
2179:**Example `CallDetail` (extends `TopCallRow`):**
2180:```ts
2181:{
2182:  ...TopCallRow,
2183:  idempotencyKey: "...",
2184:  providerRequestId: "req_011CaEL8o...",
2185:  organisationId: "8b2e...",      // null for overhead rows (system / analyzer)
2186:  subaccountId: "a14f...",        // null for overhead rows and org-scoped work without a subaccount
2187:  runId: "...",                   // if sourceType = 'agent_run'; null otherwise
2188:  sourceId: null,                 // uuid for analyzer (= skill_analyzer_jobs.id per §6.3); null for other source types
2189:  attemptNumber: 1,
2190:  fallbackChain: null,            // parsed JSON or null
2191:  errorMessage: null,
2192:  parseFailureRawExcerpt: null,
2193:  abortReason: null,
2194:  cachedPromptTokens: 0,
2195:  providerLatencyMs: 47200,
2196:  routerOverheadMs: 12,
2197:}
2198:```
2199:
2200:**Link-target nullability (load-bearing for the §11.6 drawer links):**
2201:- `organisationId` / `subaccountId` — null when the corresponding `…Name` field is null (i.e. overhead rows where no org/subaccount applies). Drawer renders the link row only when both the name and the id are non-null.
2202:- `runId` — non-null iff `sourceType = 'agent_run'`; the drawer's "Originating run" link renders only for agent rows.
2203:- `sourceId` — non-null for `sourceType ∈ {'analyzer'}` (joins to `skill_analyzer_jobs.id`); `null` for other source types today. Drawer's "Originating job" link renders only when non-null.
2204:
2205:**Producer:** `systemPnlService.getTopCalls()` / `.getCallDetail()`.
2206:**Consumer:** `PnlTopCallsList.tsx` / `PnlCallDetailDrawer.tsx`.
2207:
2208:### 19.7 `ParseFailureError`
2209:
2210:**Type:** TypeScript class, declared in `server/lib/parseFailureError.ts` (new).
2211:
2212:```ts
2213:export class ParseFailureError extends Error {
2214:  code = 'CLASSIFICATION_PARSE_FAILURE' as const;
2215:  rawExcerpt: string;
2216:  constructor(args: { rawExcerpt: string }) {
2217:    super('LLM response failed post-processing schema check');
2218:    this.rawExcerpt = args.rawExcerpt;
2219:  }
2220:}
2221:```
2222:
2223:**Producer:** caller-side post-processor (e.g. analyzer's `parseClassificationResponseWithMerge` wrapper).
2224:**Consumer:** `llmRouter.routeCall()` catches, writes the `llm_requests` row with `status='parse_failure'` and `parseFailureRawExcerpt = err.rawExcerpt`, then re-throws for caller control flow.
2225:
2226:### 19.8 `ArchiveResult`
2227:
2228:**Type:** TypeScript, declared in `server/jobs/llmLedgerArchiveJob.ts`.
2229:
2230:```ts
2231:{
2232:  totalMoved: 47213,
2233:  cutoff: "2025-04-20T03:00:00.000Z",
2234:}
2235:```
2236:
2237:**Producer:** `archiveOldLedgerRows()`.
2238:**Consumer:** pg-boss job completion log; logged via `logger.info('llm_ledger_archive_complete', result)`.
2239:
2240:### 19.9 HTTP API payloads
2241:
2242:All endpoints in §11.3 return JSON with a wrapper:
2243:
2244:```ts
2245:{
2246:  "data": <typed payload per endpoint>,
2247:  "meta": {
2248:    "period": "2026-04",
2249:    "generatedAt": "2026-04-20T14:42:00.000Z",
2250:    "ledgerRowsScanned": 1284029
2251:  }
2252:}
2253:```
2254:
2255:Error responses follow the existing app convention (`{ statusCode, message, errorCode }`).
2256:
2257:### 19.10 `budgetService.checkAndReserve()` return type (widened)
2258:
2259:**Type:** TypeScript, declared in `server/services/budgetService.ts`.
2260:
2261:**Signature after this spec:**
2262:
2263:```ts
2264:async function checkAndReserve(
2265:  ctx: LLMCallContext,
2266:  conn?: TxOrDb
2267:): Promise<string | null>
2268:```
2269:
2270:**Semantics:**
2271:
2272:- Returns a reservation id (`string`) for caller paths that ARE budgeted — i.e. `sourceType ∈ {'agent_run', 'process_execution', 'iee'}`. Callers are expected to release the reservation on error or commit on success.
2273:- Returns `null` for caller paths that are NOT budgeted — i.e. `sourceType ∈ {'system', 'analyzer'}`. The router treats `null` as "no reservation to release, no budget math to unwind."
2274:
2275:**Producer:** `budgetService.checkAndReserve()`.
2276:**Consumer:** `llmRouter.routeCall()` — the only caller of the budget service, branches on whether the returned id is null vs string for release semantics.
2277:
2278:**Back-compat note:** the current signature returns `string` unconditionally (throws `BudgetExceededError` for failure). Widening to `string | null` is a non-breaking change for all existing typed callers because none of them narrow the return beyond `string`; `null` is only returned on a code path that does not exist today (system/analyzer).
2279:

1762:
1763:## 17. Deferred items
1764:
1765:Per §7 of the spec-authoring checklist, every "deferred" / "later" / "future" reference in prose must have an entry here.
1766:
1767:- **Detail drawer rich-state interactions.** P4 ships the base drawer (fields + copy buttons + close). Rich state — filter-by-request-ID inline, keyboard navigation, cross-reference search, embedded link to run/job with deep context — is deferred. Reason: scope discipline on P4, which is already the largest single PR.
1768:- **Auto-archival of `cost_aggregates` rows older than 24 months.** Deferred. Reason: rollups are tiny (thousands of rows vs millions on the ledger); no operational need.
1769:- **Per-org retention overrides in `llm_requests`.** Deferred. Reason: no commercial customer has requested >12-month retention; adding per-org config would require new config tables + UI, out of scope for the ledger-generalisation work.
1770:- **Provider-level cost reconciliation (compare our `cost_raw` to Anthropic invoice exports).** Deferred. Reason: requires invoice-parsing infrastructure; the System P&L page gives us internal cost totals which is sufficient for this spec's goals.
1771:- **Anomaly alerting on System P&L metrics** ("Platform overhead >15% of revenue for 3 consecutive days", "Org X's net margin dropped below 10%"). Deferred. Reason: alerting infrastructure is a separate concern; page-only surfacing in P4 is the right stop-point.
1772:- **Shared `useLedgerQuery` hook on the client** for consistent data fetching across the P&L page. Deferred. Reason: P4 uses React Query with per-component keys; a shared hook is a refactor candidate once the page is stable, not a day-one requirement.
1773:- **Cross-org cost trend tuning** (smoothing, seasonality overlays, year-over-year comparison). Deferred. Reason: the 30-day line chart in P4 is sufficient for CEO-level reporting; advanced chart work is a follow-up.
1774:- **Direct-adapter caller audit of callers outside the analyzer subsystem.** P2 produces the audit document; P3 migrates the entire analyzer subsystem (both `server/jobs/skillAnalyzerJob.ts` and `server/services/skillAnalyzerService.ts`) as proof-of-concept. Callers outside the analyzer subsystem — e.g. workspace-memory, belief-extraction, and any other confirmed by P2 — are migrated in a follow-up spec. Reason: scope containment — this spec proves the pattern on one subsystem; the pattern, once proven, can be applied elsewhere without a new design.
1775:- **Real destinations for the System P&L page footer links (`Margin policies`, `Retention`, `Billing rules`).** P4 renders these as decorative `<span>` elements per §11.4.1. Candidates for real destinations: an admin `Margin policies` page (org-by-org override tables), an admin `Retention` page exposing `env.LLM_LEDGER_RETENTION_MONTHS`, and an admin `Billing rules` page (invoice generation, per-client billing periods). Reason: each destination is its own admin page that does not yet exist; wiring real hrefs into P4 would balloon scope from a single admin surface into a multi-page suite.
1776:- **User-initiated cancel wiring for analyzer LLM calls (`caller_cancel`).** §8.1's abort-reason mechanism supports both `caller_timeout` and `caller_cancel`, but this spec only wires the timeout path in §10.1. Threading a UI/job-level cancel into the analyzer's `AbortController` requires a new cancel-propagation hook (UI → pg-boss job cancel → analyzer worker → `AbortController.abort('caller_cancel')`) that does not exist today. Reason for deferral: the analyzer pg-boss job has no UI-cancel surface today; adding one is its own scope (cancellable long-running jobs) and out of this spec's ledger-generalisation work. The schema-level `abort_reason = 'caller_cancel'` value stays listed in the CHECK constraint so no future migration is needed when the wiring lands.
1777:
1778:---
1779:
1780:## 18. Rollout
1781:
1782:### 18.1 Commit-and-revert posture
1783:
1784:Per `docs/spec-context.md`: `rollout_model: commit_and_revert`. No staged rollout, no feature flags, no percentage-based traffic shifting.
1785:
1786:Each phase ships as a single PR to `main`. If a phase breaks something, revert the PR and fix forward in the next PR. `pre_production: yes` means no live users to protect.
1787:
1788:### 18.2 Rollback decision matrix
1789:
1790:| Phase | Rollback cost | Rollback plan |
1791:|---|---|---|
1792:| P1 | Low | Revert migration via a 0180_rollback.sql; revert code PR |
1793:| P2 | Zero | Revert gate registration; no code or schema change |
1794:| P3 | Low | Revert the `skillAnalyzerJob.ts` PR; analyzer falls back to direct-adapter path; re-add analyzer to gate whitelist |
1795:| P4 | Zero | Revert UI PR; no data or schema dependency to roll back |
1796:| P5 | Medium | Revert archive job registration; `llm_requests_archive` table can stay (empty cost to retain) |
1797:
1798:P5's rollback cost is medium because if the archive job has already run, rows are in the archive table. Rolling back the job doesn't move them back automatically — a separate data-repair step would be needed. Mitigation: verify P5 on a dev DB with synthetic data before merging.
1799:
1800:### 18.3 Pre-launch checklist
1801:
1802:Before merging P3 (the highest-impact phase):
1803:
1804:- [ ] All P1 migrations applied to dev DB and basic shape verified
1805:- [ ] `verify-no-direct-adapter-calls.sh` runs locally and exits correctly on both sides (red before P3, green after)
1806:- [ ] Skill-analyzer import runs end-to-end on dev
1807:- [ ] One ledger row manually inspected and matched against Anthropic console
1808:- [ ] `pr-reviewer` has passed on the PR
1809:- [ ] No TypeScript errors from schema type regen
1810:- [ ] `npm run lint` clean
1811:- [ ] `npm run build` clean
1812:
1813:Before merging P4:
1814:
1815:- [ ] Same as above for UI PR
1816:- [ ] All 4 tabs render with real (analyzer-post-P3) data
1817:- [ ] Permission gate verified (non-admin gets 403)
1818:- [ ] No console errors on page load
1819:
1820:### 18.4 Documentation-sync step (required per `CLAUDE.md §11`)
1821:
1822:Every phase's PR includes the doc updates listed in §14.9. Specifically:
1823:
1824:- P1: `architecture.md` LLM ledger section
1825:- P3: `CLAUDE.md` key files table (add analyzer routing pointer)
1826:- P4: `CLAUDE.md` key files table (add System P&L); `docs/capabilities.md` Agency Capabilities section
1827:- P5: `CLAUDE.md` key files table (add ledger-archive job); `architecture.md` retention section
1828:
1829:Not "in a follow-up PR" — in the same commit as the code change.
1830:

1833:## 19. Contracts (appendix)
1834:
1835:Every data shape crossing a service boundary, per §3 of the spec-authoring checklist. Each contract includes name, type, example, nullability/defaults, producer, and consumer.
1836:
1837:### 19.1 `LLMCallContext` (extended)
1838:
1839:**Type:** TypeScript / Zod, declared in `server/services/llmRouter.ts`.
1840:
1841:**Example instance (analyzer classify call):**
1842:```ts
1843:{
1844:  organisationId: "8b2e1a9c-3f54-4e0a-a111-b2d7e9f0a1b2",
1845:  sourceType: "analyzer",
1846:  sourceId: "c7d3f012-4a55-4f1a-c222-b8f0d1e3c4b5",
1847:  featureTag: "skill-analyzer-classify",
1848:  taskType: "general",
1849:  executionPhase: null,
1850:  systemCallerPolicy: "bypass_routing",
1851:  provider: "anthropic",
1852:  model: "claude-sonnet-4-6",
1853:  abortSignal: <AbortSignal>,
1854:}
1855:```
1856:
1857:**Nullability (matches the CHECK constraint in §6.1):**
1858:- `sourceId`:
1859:  - **Required** when `sourceType = 'analyzer'`.
1860:  - **Optional** when `sourceType = 'system'` (may be NULL for truly unattributable platform work, or set to a job/service identifier when attribution exists).
1861:  - **Must be NULL** when `sourceType ∈ {'agent_run', 'process_execution', 'iee'}` — those rows use the typed FKs instead.
1862:- `featureTag`: strongly recommended, defaults to `'unknown'` with a warning log from the router.
1863:- `executionPhase`: NULL for `analyzer` and `system`; required for `agent_run`, `process_execution`, `iee`.
1864:- `abortSignal`: optional; absence is treated as "no caller-side cancellation support."
1865:
1866:**Producer:** every caller of `llmRouter.routeCall()`.
1867:**Consumer:** `llmRouter.ts` internal; not persisted directly (fields land on `llm_requests` row columns).
1868:
1869:### 19.2 `llm_requests` row (post-migration 0180)
1870:
1871:**Type:** Drizzle table row, declared in `server/db/schema/llmRequests.ts`.
1872:
1873:**Example instance (analyzer classify success):**
1874:```json
1875:{
1876:  "id": "row-uuid",
1877:  "idempotencyKey": "8b2e1a9c-...:c7d3f012-...:skill-analyzer-classify:general:anthropic:claude-sonnet-4-6:<messagehash>",
1878:  "organisationId": "8b2e1a9c-3f54-4e0a-a111-b2d7e9f0a1b2",
1879:  "subaccountId": null,
1880:  "sourceType": "analyzer",
1881:  "sourceId": "c7d3f012-4a55-4f1a-c222-b8f0d1e3c4b5",
1882:  "featureTag": "skill-analyzer-classify",
1883:  "runId": null, "executionId": null, "ieeRunId": null,
1884:  "taskType": "general",
1885:  "executionPhase": null,
1886:  "provider": "anthropic",
1887:  "model": "claude-sonnet-4-6",
1888:  "providerRequestId": "req_011CaEL8oXSaxjj9ZT1gC2Ai",
1889:  "tokensIn": 7252, "tokensOut": 4819, "cachedPromptTokens": 0,
1890:  "costRaw": "0.04181900",
1891:  "costWithMargin": "0.04181900",
1892:  "costWithMarginCents": 4,
1893:  "marginMultiplier": "1.0000",
1894:  "providerLatencyMs": 47200,
1895:  "routerOverheadMs": 12,
1896:  "status": "success",
1897:  "attemptNumber": 1,
1898:  "parseFailureRawExcerpt": null,
1899:  "abortReason": null,
1900:  "billingMonth": "2026-04",
1901:  "billingDay": "2026-04-20",
1902:  "createdAt": "2026-04-20T03:38:22.102Z"
1903:}
1904:```
1905:
1906:**Example instance (analyzer classify aborted by caller):**
1907:```json
1908:{
1909:  "sourceType": "analyzer",
1910:  "sourceId": "c7d3f012-...",
1911:  "featureTag": "skill-analyzer-classify",
1912:  "tokensIn": 7252, "tokensOut": null,
1913:  "costRaw": "0",
1914:  "costWithMargin": "0",
1915:  "status": "aborted_by_caller",
1916:  "abortReason": "caller_cancel",
1917:  "parseFailureRawExcerpt": null,
1918:  "errorMessage": "Request aborted by caller (caller_cancel)"
1919:}
1920:```
1921:
1922:Note: `status = 'aborted_by_caller'` here because our side fired `AbortController.abort()`. A `client_disconnected` row would result from a mid-body network RST where we did not initiate the abort — see §6.4 for the full mapping.
1923:
1924:Note: analyzer rows use `marginMultiplier: "1.0000"` because system-level work doesn't add margin — cost equals revenue for these (which is to say, there is no revenue; the row just records cost). The router enforces this override at insert time per §7.4.
1925:
1926:**Producer:** `llmRouter.routeCall()` is the only writer.
1927:**Consumer:** `systemPnlService`, `llmUsageService`, `costAggregateService`.
1928:
1929:### 19.3 `PnlSummary`
1930:
1931:**Type:** TypeScript, declared in `server/services/systemPnlService.ts` and `shared/types/systemPnl.ts` (to share with the client).
1932:
1933:**Example:**
1934:```ts
1935:{
1936:  period: "2026-04",
1937:  previousPeriod: "2026-03",
1938:  revenue: { cents: 2720690, change: { pct: 11.8, direction: "up" } },
1939:  grossProfit: { cents: 561413, margin: 20.6, change: { pct: 7.4, direction: "up" } },
1940:  platformOverhead: { cents: 188742, pctOfRevenue: 6.9 },
1941:  netProfit: { cents: 372671, margin: 13.7, change: { pp: 0.4, direction: "up" } },
1942:}
1943:```
1944:
1945:**Nullability:** `previousPeriod` data may be null if there's no prior period. Change indicators are then `null`.
1946:
1947:**Producer:** `systemPnlService.getPnlSummary()`.
1948:**Consumer:** `PnlKpiCard.tsx`.
1949:
1950:### 19.4 `OrgRow`
1951:
1952:**Type:** TypeScript, shared.
1953:
1954:**Example:**
1955:```ts
1956:{
1957:  organisationId: "8b2e...",
1958:  organisationName: "Summit Digital",
1959:  slug: "summit-digital",
1960:  marginTier: 1.40,
1961:  subaccountCount: 14,
1962:  requests: 291482,
1963:  revenueCents: 759693,
1964:  costCents: 542638,
1965:  profitCents: 217055,
1966:  marginPct: 28.6,
1967:  pctOfRevenue: 27.9,
1968:  trendSparkline: [0.8, 0.82, 0.85, ...30 values...],
1969:}
1970:```
1971:
1972:**Nullability:** none — platform-admin view aggregates always return populated rows.
1973:
1974:**Producer:** `systemPnlService.getByOrganisation()`. The method returns `{ orgs: OrgRow[]; overhead: OverheadRow }`: the per-org rows plus a single synthetic aggregated overhead row (see `OverheadRow` below). The client renders `overhead` as the bottom-of-table indigo row per `prototypes/system-costs-page.html` lines 534-560.
1975:
1976:**Consumer:** `PnlByOrganisationTable.tsx`.
1977:
1978:**`OverheadRow` contract (new, shared):**
1979:```ts
1980:{
1981:  kind: "overhead";
1982:  label: "Platform background work";
1983:  description: string;            // e.g. "System + analyzer (see By Source Type for split)"
1984:  requests: number;
1985:  revenueCents: null;
1986:  costCents: number;
1987:  profitCents: number;            // = -costCents
1988:  marginPct: null;
1989:  pctOfRevenue: number;
1990:}
1991:```
1992:Reused by every tab that renders an aggregated overhead row (today: `By Organisation` only). `By Source Type` uses a separate `SourceTypeRow` per §19.5 because the overhead there is split into two distinct rows.
1993:
1994:### 19.5 Per-tab row contracts
1995:
1996:Each tab's row type has its own explicit shape in `shared/types/systemPnl.ts`. The shape family is similar to `OrgRow` for the money columns, but the identity columns and the tab-specific columns differ per tab.
1997:
1998:#### 19.5.1 `SubacctRow`
1999:
2000:**Type:** TypeScript, declared in `shared/types/systemPnl.ts`.

1756:
1757:- End-to-end P&L page flows (framing excludes E2E).
1758:- Idempotency behaviour of the archive job under concurrent runs (framing: `migration_safety_tests: defer_until_live_data_exists`).
1759:- Load tests on `cost_aggregates` upsert path (framing: `performance_baselines: defer_until_production`).
1760:
1761:---
1762:
1763:## 17. Deferred items
1764:
1765:Per §7 of the spec-authoring checklist, every "deferred" / "later" / "future" reference in prose must have an entry here.
1766:
1767:- **Detail drawer rich-state interactions.** P4 ships the base drawer (fields + copy buttons + close). Rich state — filter-by-request-ID inline, keyboard navigation, cross-reference search, embedded link to run/job with deep context — is deferred. Reason: scope discipline on P4, which is already the largest single PR.
1768:- **Auto-archival of `cost_aggregates` rows older than 24 months.** Deferred. Reason: rollups are tiny (thousands of rows vs millions on the ledger); no operational need.
1769:- **Per-org retention overrides in `llm_requests`.** Deferred. Reason: no commercial customer has requested >12-month retention; adding per-org config would require new config tables + UI, out of scope for the ledger-generalisation work.
1770:- **Provider-level cost reconciliation (compare our `cost_raw` to Anthropic invoice exports).** Deferred. Reason: requires invoice-parsing infrastructure; the System P&L page gives us internal cost totals which is sufficient for this spec's goals.
1771:- **Anomaly alerting on System P&L metrics** ("Platform overhead >15% of revenue for 3 consecutive days", "Org X's net margin dropped below 10%"). Deferred. Reason: alerting infrastructure is a separate concern; page-only surfacing in P4 is the right stop-point.
1772:- **Shared `useLedgerQuery` hook on the client** for consistent data fetching across the P&L page. Deferred. Reason: P4 uses React Query with per-component keys; a shared hook is a refactor candidate once the page is stable, not a day-one requirement.
1773:- **Cross-org cost trend tuning** (smoothing, seasonality overlays, year-over-year comparison). Deferred. Reason: the 30-day line chart in P4 is sufficient for CEO-level reporting; advanced chart work is a follow-up.
1774:- **Direct-adapter caller audit of callers outside the analyzer subsystem.** P2 produces the audit document; P3 migrates the entire analyzer subsystem (both `server/jobs/skillAnalyzerJob.ts` and `server/services/skillAnalyzerService.ts`) as proof-of-concept. Callers outside the analyzer subsystem — e.g. workspace-memory, belief-extraction, and any other confirmed by P2 — are migrated in a follow-up spec. Reason: scope containment — this spec proves the pattern on one subsystem; the pattern, once proven, can be applied elsewhere without a new design.
1775:- **Real destinations for the System P&L page footer links (`Margin policies`, `Retention`, `Billing rules`).** P4 renders these as decorative `<span>` elements per §11.4.1. Candidates for real destinations: an admin `Margin policies` page (org-by-org override tables), an admin `Retention` page exposing `env.LLM_LEDGER_RETENTION_MONTHS`, and an admin `Billing rules` page (invoice generation, per-client billing periods). Reason: each destination is its own admin page that does not yet exist; wiring real hrefs into P4 would balloon scope from a single admin surface into a multi-page suite.
1776:- **User-initiated cancel wiring for analyzer LLM calls (`caller_cancel`).** §8.1's abort-reason mechanism supports both `caller_timeout` and `caller_cancel`, but this spec only wires the timeout path in §10.1. Threading a UI/job-level cancel into the analyzer's `AbortController` requires a new cancel-propagation hook (UI → pg-boss job cancel → analyzer worker → `AbortController.abort('caller_cancel')`) that does not exist today. Reason for deferral: the analyzer pg-boss job has no UI-cancel surface today; adding one is its own scope (cancellable long-running jobs) and out of this spec's ledger-generalisation work. The schema-level `abort_reason = 'caller_cancel'` value stays listed in the CHECK constraint so no future migration is needed when the wiring lands.
1777:
1778:---
1779:
1780:## 18. Rollout
1781:
1782:### 18.1 Commit-and-revert posture
1783:
1784:Per `docs/spec-context.md`: `rollout_model: commit_and_revert`. No staged rollout, no feature flags, no percentage-based traffic shifting.
1785:
1786:Each phase ships as a single PR to `main`. If a phase breaks something, revert the PR and fix forward in the next PR. `pre_production: yes` means no live users to protect.
1787:
1788:### 18.2 Rollback decision matrix
1789:
1790:| Phase | Rollback cost | Rollback plan |
1791:|---|---|---|
1792:| P1 | Low | Revert migration via a 0180_rollback.sql; revert code PR |
1793:| P2 | Zero | Revert gate registration; no code or schema change |
1794:| P3 | Low | Revert the `skillAnalyzerJob.ts` PR; analyzer falls back to direct-adapter path; re-add analyzer to gate whitelist |
1795:| P4 | Zero | Revert UI PR; no data or schema dependency to roll back |
1796:| P5 | Medium | Revert archive job registration; `llm_requests_archive` table can stay (empty cost to retain) |
1797:
1798:P5's rollback cost is medium because if the archive job has already run, rows are in the archive table. Rolling back the job doesn't move them back automatically — a separate data-repair step would be needed. Mitigation: verify P5 on a dev DB with synthetic data before merging.
1799:
1800:### 18.3 Pre-launch checklist
1801:
1802:Before merging P3 (the highest-impact phase):
1803:
1804:- [ ] All P1 migrations applied to dev DB and basic shape verified
1805:- [ ] `verify-no-direct-adapter-calls.sh` runs locally and exits correctly on both sides (red before P3, green after)
1806:- [ ] Skill-analyzer import runs end-to-end on dev
1807:- [ ] One ledger row manually inspected and matched against Anthropic console
1808:- [ ] `pr-reviewer` has passed on the PR
1809:- [ ] No TypeScript errors from schema type regen
1810:- [ ] `npm run lint` clean
1811:- [ ] `npm run build` clean
1812:
1813:Before merging P4:
1814:
1815:- [ ] Same as above for UI PR
1816:- [ ] All 4 tabs render with real (analyzer-post-P3) data
1817:- [ ] Permission gate verified (non-admin gets 403)
1818:- [ ] No console errors on page load
1819:
1820:### 18.4 Documentation-sync step (required per `CLAUDE.md §11`)
1821:
1822:Every phase's PR includes the doc updates listed in §14.9. Specifically:
1823:
1824:- P1: `architecture.md` LLM ledger section
1825:- P3: `CLAUDE.md` key files table (add analyzer routing pointer)
1826:- P4: `CLAUDE.md` key files table (add System P&L); `docs/capabilities.md` Agency Capabilities section
1827:- P5: `CLAUDE.md` key files table (add ledger-archive job); `architecture.md` retention section
1828:
1829:Not "in a follow-up PR" — in the same commit as the code change.
1830:
1831:---
1832:
1833:## 19. Contracts (appendix)
1834:
1835:Every data shape crossing a service boundary, per §3 of the spec-authoring checklist. Each contract includes name, type, example, nullability/defaults, producer, and consumer.
1836:
1837:### 19.1 `LLMCallContext` (extended)
1838:
1839:**Type:** TypeScript / Zod, declared in `server/services/llmRouter.ts`.
1840:
1841:**Example instance (analyzer classify call):**
1842:```ts
1843:{
1844:  organisationId: "8b2e1a9c-3f54-4e0a-a111-b2d7e9f0a1b2",
1845:  sourceType: "analyzer",
1846:  sourceId: "c7d3f012-4a55-4f1a-c222-b8f0d1e3c4b5",
1847:  featureTag: "skill-analyzer-classify",
1848:  taskType: "general",
1849:  executionPhase: null,
1850:  systemCallerPolicy: "bypass_routing",
1851:  provider: "anthropic",
1852:  model: "claude-sonnet-4-6",
1853:  abortSignal: <AbortSignal>,
1854:}
1855:```
1856:
1857:**Nullability (matches the CHECK constraint in §6.1):**
1858:- `sourceId`:
1859:  - **Required** when `sourceType = 'analyzer'`.
1860:  - **Optional** when `sourceType = 'system'` (may be NULL for truly unattributable platform work, or set to a job/service identifier when attribution exists).
1861:  - **Must be NULL** when `sourceType ∈ {'agent_run', 'process_execution', 'iee'}` — those rows use the typed FKs instead.
1862:- `featureTag`: strongly recommended, defaults to `'unknown'` with a warning log from the router.
1863:- `executionPhase`: NULL for `analyzer` and `system`; required for `agent_run`, `process_execution`, `iee`.
1864:- `abortSignal`: optional; absence is treated as "no caller-side cancellation support."
1865:
1866:**Producer:** every caller of `llmRouter.routeCall()`.
1867:**Consumer:** `llmRouter.ts` internal; not persisted directly (fields land on `llm_requests` row columns).
1868:
1869:### 19.2 `llm_requests` row (post-migration 0180)
1870:
1871:**Type:** Drizzle table row, declared in `server/db/schema/llmRequests.ts`.
1872:
1873:**Example instance (analyzer classify success):**
1874:```json
1875:{
1876:  "id": "row-uuid",
1877:  "idempotencyKey": "8b2e1a9c-...:c7d3f012-...:skill-analyzer-classify:general:anthropic:claude-sonnet-4-6:<messagehash>",
1878:  "organisationId": "8b2e1a9c-3f54-4e0a-a111-b2d7e9f0a1b2",
1879:  "subaccountId": null,
1880:  "sourceType": "analyzer",
1881:  "sourceId": "c7d3f012-4a55-4f1a-c222-b8f0d1e3c4b5",
1882:  "featureTag": "skill-analyzer-classify",
1883:  "runId": null, "executionId": null, "ieeRunId": null,
1884:  "taskType": "general",
1885:  "executionPhase": null,
1886:  "provider": "anthropic",
1887:  "model": "claude-sonnet-4-6",
1888:  "providerRequestId": "req_011CaEL8oXSaxjj9ZT1gC2Ai",
1889:  "tokensIn": 7252, "tokensOut": 4819, "cachedPromptTokens": 0,
1890:  "costRaw": "0.04181900",
1891:  "costWithMargin": "0.04181900",
1892:  "costWithMarginCents": 4,
1893:  "marginMultiplier": "1.0000",
1894:  "providerLatencyMs": 47200,
1895:  "routerOverheadMs": 12,
1896:  "status": "success",
1897:  "attemptNumber": 1,
1898:  "parseFailureRawExcerpt": null,
1899:  "abortReason": null,
1900:  "billingMonth": "2026-04",
1901:  "billingDay": "2026-04-20",
1902:  "createdAt": "2026-04-20T03:38:22.102Z"
1903:}
1904:```
1905:
1906:**Example instance (analyzer classify aborted by caller):**
1907:```json
1908:{
1909:  "sourceType": "analyzer",
1910:  "sourceId": "c7d3f012-...",
1911:  "featureTag": "skill-analyzer-classify",
1912:  "tokensIn": 7252, "tokensOut": null,
1913:  "costRaw": "0",
1914:  "costWithMargin": "0",
1915:  "status": "aborted_by_caller",
1916:  "abortReason": "caller_cancel",
1917:  "parseFailureRawExcerpt": null,
1918:  "errorMessage": "Request aborted by caller (caller_cancel)"
1919:}
1920:```
1921:
1922:Note: `status = 'aborted_by_caller'` here because our side fired `AbortController.abort()`. A `client_disconnected` row would result from a mid-body network RST where we did not initiate the abort — see §6.4 for the full mapping.
1923:
1924:Note: analyzer rows use `marginMultiplier: "1.0000"` because system-level work doesn't add margin — cost equals revenue for these (which is to say, there is no revenue; the row just records cost). The router enforces this override at insert time per §7.4.
1925:
1926:**Producer:** `llmRouter.routeCall()` is the only writer.
1927:**Consumer:** `systemPnlService`, `llmUsageService`, `costAggregateService`.
1928:
1929:### 19.3 `PnlSummary`
1930:
1931:**Type:** TypeScript, declared in `server/services/systemPnlService.ts` and `shared/types/systemPnl.ts` (to share with the client).
1932:
1933:**Example:**
1934:```ts
1935:{
1936:  period: "2026-04",
1937:  previousPeriod: "2026-03",
1938:  revenue: { cents: 2720690, change: { pct: 11.8, direction: "up" } },
1939:  grossProfit: { cents: 561413, margin: 20.6, change: { pct: 7.4, direction: "up" } },
1940:  platformOverhead: { cents: 188742, pctOfRevenue: 6.9 },
1941:  netProfit: { cents: 372671, margin: 13.7, change: { pp: 0.4, direction: "up" } },
1942:}
1943:```
1944:
1945:**Nullability:** `previousPeriod` data may be null if there's no prior period. Change indicators are then `null`.
1946:
1947:**Producer:** `systemPnlService.getPnlSummary()`.
1948:**Consumer:** `PnlKpiCard.tsx`.
1949:
1950:### 19.4 `OrgRow`
1951:
1952:**Type:** TypeScript, shared.
1953:
1954:**Example:**
1955:```ts
1956:{
1957:  organisationId: "8b2e...",
1958:  organisationName: "Summit Digital",
1959:  slug: "summit-digital",
1960:  marginTier: 1.40,
1961:  subaccountCount: 14,
1962:  requests: 291482,
1963:  revenueCents: 759693,
1964:  costCents: 542638,
1965:  profitCents: 217055,
1966:  marginPct: 28.6,
1967:  pctOfRevenue: 27.9,
1968:  trendSparkline: [0.8, 0.82, 0.85, ...30 values...],
1969:}
1970:```
1971:
1972:**Nullability:** none — platform-admin view aggregates always return populated rows.
1973:
1974:**Producer:** `systemPnlService.getByOrganisation()`. The method returns `{ orgs: OrgRow[]; overhead: OverheadRow }`: the per-org rows plus a single synthetic aggregated overhead row (see `OverheadRow` below). The client renders `overhead` as the bottom-of-table indigo row per `prototypes/system-costs-page.html` lines 534-560.
1975:
1976:**Consumer:** `PnlByOrganisationTable.tsx`.
1977:
1978:**`OverheadRow` contract (new, shared):**
1979:```ts
1980:{
1981:  kind: "overhead";
1982:  label: "Platform background work";
1983:  description: string;            // e.g. "System + analyzer (see By Source Type for split)"
1984:  requests: number;
1985:  revenueCents: null;
1986:  costCents: number;
1987:  profitCents: number;            // = -costCents
1988:  marginPct: null;
1989:  pctOfRevenue: number;
1990:}
1991:```
1992:Reused by every tab that renders an aggregated overhead row (today: `By Organisation` only). `By Source Type` uses a separate `SourceTypeRow` per §19.5 because the overhead there is split into two distinct rows.
1993:
1994:### 19.5 Per-tab row contracts
1995:
1996:Each tab's row type has its own explicit shape in `shared/types/systemPnl.ts`. The shape family is similar to `OrgRow` for the money columns, but the identity columns and the tab-specific columns differ per tab.
1997:
1998:#### 19.5.1 `SubacctRow`
1999:
2000:**Type:** TypeScript, declared in `shared/types/systemPnl.ts`.

1166:      document.querySelectorAll('.tab-view').forEach(v => v.classList.remove('active'));
1167:      document.getElementById('view-' + tab).classList.add('active');
1168:      const status = document.getElementById('tab-status');
1169:      if (status) status.innerHTML = TAB_STATUS[tab];
1170:    });
1171:  });
1172:
1173:  // Organisation column dropdown (open on page load for review)
1174:  const dd = document.querySelector('.dropdown-open');
1175:  if (dd) {
1176:    const btn = dd.querySelector('button');
1177:    const panel = dd.querySelector('.dd-panel');
1178:    btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
1179:      e.stopPropagation();
1180:      dd.classList.toggle('dropdown-open');
1181:      panel.style.display = dd.classList.contains('dropdown-open') ? '' : 'none';
1182:    });
1183:    document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
1184:      if (!dd.contains(e.target)) {
1185:        dd.classList.remove('dropdown-open');
1186:        panel.style.display = 'none';
1187:      }
1188:    });
1189:  }
1190:</script>
1191:
1192:</body>
1193:</html>
